No provider-specific `discord` tool exposed to the agent.\n\n## Musts\n\n- Always: `channel: \"discord\"`.\n- Respect gating: `channels.discord.actions.*` (some default off: `roles`, `moderation`, `presence`, `channels`).\n- Prefer explicit ids: `guildId`, `channelId`, `messageId`, `userId`.\n- Multi-account: optional `accountId`.\n\n## Guidelines\n\n- Avoid Markdown tables in outbound Discord messages.\n- Mention users as `<@USER_ID>`.\n- Prefer Discord components v2 (`components`) for rich UI; use legacy `embeds` only when you must.\n\n## Targets\n\n- Send-like actions: `to: \"channel:<id>\"` or `to: \"user:<id>\"`.\n- Message-specific actions: `channelId: \"<id>\"` (or `to`) + `messageId: \"<id>\"`.\n\n## Common Actions (Examples)\n\nSend message:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"send\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"to\": \"channel:123\",\n  \"message\": \"hello\",\n  \"silent\": true\n}\n```\n\nSend with media:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"send\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"to\": \"channel:123\",\n  \"message\": \"see attachment\",\n  \"media\": \"file:///tmp/example.png\"\n}\n```\n\n- Optional `silent: true` to suppress Discord notifications.\n\nSend with components v2 (recommended for rich UI):\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"send\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"to\": \"channel:123\",\n  \"message\": \"Status update\",\n  \"components\": \"[Carbon v2 components]\"\n}\n```\n\n- `components` expects Carbon component instances (Container, TextDisplay, etc.) from JS/TS integrations.\n- Do not combine `components` with `embeds` (Discord rejects v2 + embeds).\n\nLegacy embeds (not recommended):\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"send\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"to\": \"channel:123\",\n  \"message\": \"Status update\",\n  \"embeds\": [{ \"title\": \"Legacy\", \"description\": \"Embeds are legacy.\" }]\n}\n```\n\n- `embeds` are ignored when components v2 are present.\n\nReact:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"react\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"channelId\": \"123\",\n  \"messageId\": \"456\",\n  \"emoji\": \"✅\"\n}\n```\n\nRead:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"read\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"to\": \"channel:123\",\n  \"limit\": 20\n}\n```\n\nEdit / delete:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"edit\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"channelId\": \"123\",\n  \"messageId\": \"456\",\n  \"message\": \"fixed typo\"\n}\n```\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"delete\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"channelId\": \"123\",\n  \"messageId\": \"456\"\n}\n```\n\nPoll:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"poll\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"to\": \"channel:123\",\n  \"pollQuestion\": \"Lunch?\",\n  \"pollOption\": [\"Pizza\", \"Sushi\", \"Salad\"],\n  \"pollMulti\": false,\n  \"pollDurationHours\": 24\n}\n```\n\nPins:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"pin\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"channelId\": \"123\",\n  \"messageId\": \"456\"\n}\n```\n\nThreads:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"thread-create\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"channelId\": \"123\",\n  \"messageId\": \"456\",\n  \"threadName\": \"bug triage\"\n}\n```\n\nSearch:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"search\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"guildId\": \"999\",\n  \"query\": \"release notes\",\n  \"channelIds\": [\"123\", \"456\"],\n \"status\": \"online\"\n}\n```\n\n## Writing Style (Discord)\n\n- Short, conversational, low ceremony.\n- No markdown tables.\n- Mention users as `<@USER_ID>`.\n"

The agency's ability to verify the peaceful nature of Iran's nuclear activities was described as \\\"seriously compromised.\\\"\\n\\n### December 2025 -- Intelligence Warnings and Military Preparations\\n\\nDecember 5, 2025 -- The Israeli government publicly accused [Iran](/countries/iran) of conducting weapons-design work at a previously unknown facility south of Isfahan. [Israel](/countries/israel) shared satellite imagery with allied intelligence agencies, though Iran dismissed the claims as fabricated.\\n\\nDecember 18, 2025 -- US intelligence agencies delivered a classified briefing to the White House assessing that [Iran](/countries/iran) was \\\"within months\\\" of possessing the technical capability to assemble a nuclear device. The briefing was leaked to media outlets within days, dramatically escalating public alarm.\\n\\nDecember 30, 2025 -- President Trump issued a public warning that the [United States](/countries/united-states) \\\"will not allow [Iran](/countries/iran) to become a nuclear power under any circumstances.\\\" The statement was widely interpreted as laying the political groundwork for military action.\\n\\n## Phase 2: First Strikes (January 2026)\\n\\nThe transition from diplomatic pressure to kinetic action happened faster than most analysts predicted.\\n\\n### Early January -- Israeli Strikes on Nuclear Sites\\n\\nJanuary 8, 2026 -- [Israel](/countries/israel) launched a coordinated air campaign targeting [Iran](/countries/iran)'s nuclear infrastructure.             "text": "---\nname: discord\ndescription: \"Discord ops via the message tool (channel=discord).\"\nmetadata: { \"openclaw\": { \"emoji\": \"🎮\", \"requires\": { \"config\": [\"channels.discord.token\"] } } }\nallowed-tools: [\"message\"]\n---\n\n# Discord (Via `message`)\n\nUse the `message` tool. No provider-specific `discord` tool exposed to the agent.\n\n## Musts\n\n- Always: `channel: \"discord\"`.\n- Respect gating: `channels.discord.actions.*` (some default off: `roles`, `moderation`, `presence`, `channels`).\n- Prefer explicit ids: `guildId`, `channelId`, `messageId`, `userId`.\n- Multi-account: optional `accountId`.\n\n## Guidelines\n\n- Avoid Markdown tables in outbound Discord messages.\n- Mention users as `<@USER_ID>`.\n- Prefer Discord components v2 (`components`) for rich UI; use legacy `embeds` only when you must.\n\n## Targets\n\n- Send-like actions: `to: \"channel:<id>\"` or `to: \"user:<id>\"`.\n- Message-specific actions: `channelId: \"<id>\"` (or `to`) + `messageId: \"<id>\"`.\n\n## Common Actions (Examples)\n\nSend message:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"send\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"to\": \"channel:123\",\n  \"message\": \"hello\",\n  \"silent\": true\n}\n```\n\nSend with media:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"send\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"to\": \"channel:123\",\n  \"message\": \"see attachment\",\n  \"media\": \"file:///tmp/example.png\"\n}\n```\n\n- Optional `silent: true` to suppress Discord notifications.\n\nSend with components v2 (recommended for rich UI):\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"send\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"to\": \"channel:123\",\n  \"message\": \"Status update\",\n  \"components\": \"[Carbon v2 components]\"\n}\n```\n\n- `components` expects Carbon component instances (Container, TextDisplay, etc.) from JS/TS integrations.\n- Do not combine `components` with `embeds` (Discord rejects v2 + embeds).\n\nLegacy embeds (not recommended):\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"send\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"to\": \"channel:123\",\n  \"message\": \"Status update\",\n  \"embeds\": [{ \"title\": \"Legacy\", \"description\": \"Embeds are legacy.\" }]\n}\n```\n\n- `embeds` are ignored when components v2 are present.\n\nReact:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"react\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"channelId\": \"123\",\n  \"messageId\": \"456\",\n  \"emoji\": \"✅\"\n}\n```\n\nRead:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"read\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"to\": \"channel:123\",\n  \"limit\": 20\n}\n```\n\nEdit / delete:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"edit\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"channelId\": \"123\",\n  \"messageId\": \"456\",\n  \"message\": \"fixed typo\"\n}\n```\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"delete\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"channelId\": \"123\",\n  \"messageId\": \"456\"\n}\n```\n\nPoll:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"poll\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"to\": \"channel:123\",\n  \"pollQuestion\": \"Lunch?\",\n  \"pollOption\": [\"Pizza\", \"Sushi\", \"Salad\"],\n  \"pollMulti\": false,\n  \"pollDurationHours\": 24\n}\n```\n\nPins:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"pin\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"channelId\": \"123\",\n From the collapse of diplomacy in late 2025 through Israeli strikes, the US launch of [Operation Epic Fury](/articles/us-military-buildup-middle-east-operation-epic-fury), the [assassination of Supreme Leader Khamenei](/articles/iran-supreme-leader-khamenei-killed-us-strikes), and Iran's [retaliatory strikes on US bases](/articles/iran-retaliatory-strikes-us-bases-persian-gulf), the crisis has pushed the world closer to nuclear conflict than at any point since the Cuban Missile Crisis.\\n\\nThis timeline tracks every major event, organized by phase, so readers can understand how each step led to the next.\\n\\nFor core concepts referenced throughout this timeline, see [What Is Nuclear Breakout Time](/explainers/what-is-nuclear-breakout-time)?, [What Is the IAEA](/explainers/what-is-the-iaea)?, and [What Are Proxy Wars?](/explainers/what-are-proxy-wars).\\n\\n## Phase 1: Diplomatic Collapse (October -- December 2025)\\n\\nThe groundwork for the 2026 [Iran](/countries/iran) war was laid months before the first missile launched. A series of diplomatic failures and intelligence revelations closed the remaining offramps.\\n\\n### October 2025 -- IAEA Raises the Alarm on Enrichment\\n\\nOctober 14, 2025 -- The [International Atomic Energy Agency (IAEA](/glossary#iaea)) published a quarterly report confirming that [Iran](/countries/iran) had accelerated [uranium enrichment](/glossary#enrichment) at its Fordow underground facility. Inspectors documented stockpiles enriched to 60% purity -- a short technical step from the 90% required for weapons-grade material. The IAEA Board of Governors issued a formal rebuke, but no binding action followed.\\n\\nOctober 28, 2025 -- [Iran](/countries/iran) announced expanded [centrifuge](/glossary#centrifuge) cascades at Natanz, effectively doubling [enrichment](/glossary#enrichment) capacity. [Breakout time](/glossary#breakout-time) -- the period needed to produce enough [fissile material](/glossary#fissile-material) for a single weapon -- was assessed at under two weeks by multiple Western intelligence agencies.\\n\\n### November 2025 -- JCPOA Officially Declared Dead\\n\\nNovember 12, 2025 -- After months of fruitless backchannel negotiations, the European Union's foreign policy chief formally declared the [Joint Comprehensive Plan of Action (JCPOA](/glossary#jcpoa)) \\\"no longer operative.\\\" The 2015 nuclear deal, which the US had withdrawn from under President Trump's first term in 2018, had been on life support for years. Its official death removed the last multilateral framework constraining [Iran](/countries/iran)'s nuclear program.\\n\\nNovember 20, 2025 -- The [IAEA](/glossary#iaea) Director General reported that [Iran](/countries/iran) had denied inspectors access to two undisclosed sites flagged by Western intelligence. The agency's ability to verify the peaceful nature of Iran's nuclear activities was described as \\\"seriously compromised.\\\"\\n\\n### December 2025 -- Intelligence Warnings and Military Preparations\\n\\nDecember 5, 2025 -- The Israeli government publicly accused [Iran](/countries/iran) of conducting weapons-design work at a previously unknown facility south of Isfahan. [Israel](/countries/israel) shared satellite imagery with allied intelligence agencies, though Iran dismissed the claims as fabricated.\\n\\nDecember 18, 2025 -- US intelligence agencies delivered a classified briefing to the White House assessing that [Iran](/countries/iran) was \\\"within months\\\" of possessing the technical capability to assemble a nuclear device. The briefing was leaked to media outlets within days, dramatically escalating public alarm.\\n\\nDecember 30, 2025 -- President Trump issued a public warning that the [United States](/countries/united-states) \\\"will not allow [Iran](/countries/iran) to become a nuclear power under any circumstances.\\\" The statement was widely interpreted as laying the political groundwork for military action.\\n\\n## Phase 2: First Strikes (January 2026)\\n\\nThe transition from diplomatic pressure to kinetic action happened faster than most analysts predicted.\\n\\n### Early January -- Israeli Strikes on Nuclear Sites\\n\\nJanuary 8, 2026 -- [Israel](/countries/israel) launched a coordinated air campaign targeting [Iran](/countries/iran)'s nuclear infrastructure. F-35I Adir stealth fighters, supported by US intelligence and aerial refueling, struck the Fordow [enrichment](/glossary#enrichment) facility, the Isfahan uranium conversion plant, and [centrifuge](/glossary#centrifuge) production workshops at Natanz.\\n\\nThe strikes used US-supplied [GBU-57](/glossary#gbu-57) Massive Ordnance Penetrators -- the only munitions capable of reaching Fordow's underground chambers. [Iran](/countries/iran)'s air defenses, degraded by preceding electronic warfare operations, failed to intercept the majority of incoming strikes.\\n\\nJanuary 10, 2026 -- [Iran](/countries/iran) confirmed \\\"significant damage\\\" to nuclear facilities but insisted that its program remained intact. The [IRGC](/glossary#irgc) described the strikes as \\\"an act of war requiring a decisive response.\\\"\\n\\n###\\n<<<END_EXTERNAL_UNTRUSTED_CONTENT id=\\\"6c9a55fa16a56c97\\\">>>\"\n}"

From the collapse of diplomacy in late 2025 through Israeli strikes, the US launch of [Operation Epic Fury](/articles/us-military-buildup-middle-east-operation-epic-fury), the [assassination of Supreme Leader Khamenei](/articles/iran-supreme-leader-khamenei-killed-us-strikes), and Iran's [retaliatory strikes on US bases](/articles/iran-retaliatory-strikes-us-bases-persian-gulf), the crisis has pushed the world closer to nuclear conflict than at any point since the Cuban Missile Crisis.\n\nThis timeline tracks every major event, organized by phase, so readers can understand how each step led to the next.\n\nFor core concepts referenced throughout this timeline, see [What Is Nuclear Breakout Time](/explainers/what-is-nuclear-breakout-time)?, [What Is the IAEA](/explainers/what-is-the-iaea)?, and [What Are Proxy Wars?](/explainers/what-are-proxy-wars).\n\n## Phase 1: Diplomatic Collapse (October -- December 2025)\n\nThe groundwork for the 2026 [Iran](/countries/iran) war was laid months before the first missile launched. A series of diplomatic failures and intelligence revelations closed the remaining offramps.\n\n### October 2025 -- IAEA Raises the Alarm on Enrichment\n\nOctober 14, 2025 -- The [International Atomic Energy Agency (IAEA](/glossary#iaea)) published a quarterly report confirming that [Iran](/countries/iran) had accelerated [uranium enrichment](/glossary#enrichment) at its Fordow underground facility. Inspectors documented stockpiles enriched to 60% purity -- a short technical step from the 90% required for weapons-grade material. The IAEA Board of Governors issued a formal rebuke, but no binding action followed.\n\nOctober 28, 2025 -- [Iran](/countries/iran) announced expanded [centrifuge](/glossary#centrifuge) cascades at Natanz, effectively doubling [enrichment](/glossary#enrichment) capacity. [Breakout time](/glossary#breakout-time) -- the period needed to produce enough [fissile material](/glossary#fissile-material) for a single weapon -- was assessed at under two weeks by multiple Western intelligence agencies.\n\n### November 2025 -- JCPOA Officially Declared Dead\n\nNovember 12, 2025 -- After months of fruitless backchannel negotiations, the European Union's foreign policy chief formally declared the [Joint Comprehensive Plan of Action (JCPOA](/glossary#jcpoa)) \"no longer operative.\" The 2015 nuclear deal, which the US had withdrawn from under President Trump's first term in 2018, had been on life support for years. Its official death removed the last multilateral framework constraining [Iran](/countries/iran)'s nuclear program.\n\nNovember 20, 2025 -- The [IAEA](/glossary#iaea) Director General reported that [Iran](/countries/iran) had denied inspectors access to two undisclosed sites flagged by Western intelligence. The agency's ability to verify the peaceful nature of Iran's nuclear activities was described as \"seriously compromised.\"\n\n### December 2025 -- Intelligence Warnings and Military Preparations\n\nDecember 5, 2025 -- The Israeli government publicly accused [Iran](/countries/iran) of conducting weapons-design work at a previously unknown facility south of Isfahan. [Israel](/countries/israel) shared satellite imagery with allied intelligence agencies, though Iran dismissed the claims as fabricated.\n\nDecember 18, 2025 -- US intelligence agencies delivered a classified briefing to the White House assessing that [Iran](/countries/iran) was \"within months\" of possessing the technical capability to assemble a nuclear device. The briefing was leaked to media outlets within days, dramatically escalating public alarm.\n\nDecember 30, 2025 -- President Trump issued a public warning that the [United States](/countries/united-states) \"will not allow [Iran](/countries/iran) to become a nuclear power under any circumstances.\" The statement was widely interpreted as laying the political groundwork for military action.\n\n## Phase 2: First Strikes (January 2026)\n\nThe transition from diplomatic pressure to kinetic action happened faster than most analysts predicted.\n\n### Early January -- Israeli Strikes on Nuclear Sites\n\nJanuary 8, 2026 -- [Israel](/countries/israel) launched a coordinated air campaign targeting [Iran](/countries/iran)'s nuclear infrastructure. F-35I Adir stealth fighters, supported by US intelligence and aerial refueling, struck the Fordow [enrichment](/glossary#enrichment) facility, the Isfahan uranium conversion plant, and [centrifuge](/glossary#centrifuge) production workshops at Natanz.\n\nThe strikes used US-supplied [GBU-57](/glossary#gbu-57) Massive Ordnance Penetrators -- the only munitions capable of reaching Fordow's underground chambers. [Iran](/countries/iran)'s air defenses, degraded by preceding electronic warfare operations, failed to intercept the majority of incoming strikes.\n\nJanuary 10, 2026 -- [Iran](/countries/iran) confirmed \"significant damage\" to nuclear facilities but insisted that its program remained intact. No provider-specific `discord` tool exposed to the agent.\n\n## Musts\n\n- Always: `channel: \"discord\"`.\n- Respect gating: `channels.discord.actions.*` (some default off: `roles`, `moderation`, `presence`, `channels`).\n- Prefer explicit ids: `guildId`, `channelId`, `messageId`, `userId`.\n- Multi-account: optional `accountId`.\n\n## Guidelines\n\n- Avoid Markdown tables in outbound Discord messages.\n- Mention users as `<@USER_ID>`.\n- Prefer Discord components v2 (`components`) for rich UI; use legacy `embeds` only when you must.\n\n## Targets\n\n- Send-like actions: `to: \"channel:<id>\"` or `to: \"user:<id>\"`.\n- Message-specific actions: `channelId: \"<id>\"` (or `to`) + `messageId: \"<id>\"`.\n\n## Common Actions (Examples)\n\nSend message:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"send\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"to\": \"channel:123\",\n  \"message\": \"hello\",\n  \"silent\": true\n}\n```\n\nSend with media:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"send\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"to\": \"channel:123\",\n  \"message\": \"see attachment\",\n  \"media\": \"file:///tmp/example.png\"\n}\n```\n\n- Optional `silent: true` to suppress Discord notifications.\n\nSend with components v2 (recommended for rich UI):\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"send\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"to\": \"channel:123\",\n  \"message\": \"Status update\",\n  \"components\": \"[Carbon v2 components]\"\n}\n```\n\n- `components` expects Carbon component instances (Container, TextDisplay, etc.) from JS/TS integrations.\n- Do not combine `components` with `embeds` (Discord rejects v2 + embeds).\n\nLegacy embeds (not recommended):\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"send\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"to\": \"channel:123\",\n  \"message\": \"Status update\",\n  \"embeds\": [{ \"title\": \"Legacy\", \"description\": \"Embeds are legacy.\" }]\n}\n```\n\n- `embeds` are ignored when components v2 are present.\n\nReact:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"react\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"channelId\": \"123\",\n  \"messageId\": \"456\",\n  \"emoji\": \"✅\"\n}\n```\n\nRead:\n\n```json\n{\n \"channelId\": \"123\",\n  \"messageId\": \"456\",\n  \"message\": \"fixed typo\"\n}\n```\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"delete\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"channelId\": \"123\",\n From the collapse of diplomacy in late 2025 through Israeli strikes, the US launch of [Operation Epic Fury](/articles/us-military-buildup-middle-east-operation-epic-fury), the [assassination of Supreme Leader Khamenei](/articles/iran-supreme-leader-khamenei-killed-us-strikes), and Iran's [retaliatory strikes on US bases](/articles/iran-retaliatory-strikes-us-bases-persian-gulf), the crisis has pushed the world closer to nuclear conflict than at any point since the Cuban Missile Crisis.\\n\\nThis timeline tracks every major event, organized by phase, so readers can understand how each step led to the next.\\n\\nFor core concepts referenced throughout this timeline, see [What Is Nuclear Breakout Time](/explainers/what-is-nuclear-breakout-time)?, [What Is the IAEA](/explainers/what-is-the-iaea)?, and [What Are Proxy Wars?](/explainers/what-are-proxy-wars).\\n\\n## Phase 1: Diplomatic Collapse (October -- December 2025)\\n\\nThe groundwork for the 2026 [Iran](/countries/iran) war was laid months before the first missile launched. A series of diplomatic failures and intelligence revelations closed the remaining offramps.\\n\\n### October 2025 -- IAEA Raises the Alarm on Enrichment\\n\\nOctober 14, 2025 -- The [International Atomic Energy Agency (IAEA](/glossary#iaea)) published a quarterly report confirming that [Iran](/countries/iran) had accelerated [uranium enrichment](/glossary#enrichment) at its Fordow underground facility. Inspectors documented stockpiles enriched to 60% purity -- a short technical step from the 90% required for weapons-grade material. The IAEA Board of Governors issued a formal rebuke, but no binding action followed.\\n\\nOctober 28, 2025 -- [Iran](/countries/iran) announced expanded [centrifuge](/glossary#centrifuge) cascades at Natanz, effectively doubling [enrichment](/glossary#enrichment) capacity. [Breakout time](/glossary#breakout-time) -- the period needed to produce enough [fissile material](/glossary#fissile-material) for a single weapon -- was assessed at under two weeks by multiple Western intelligence agencies.\\n\\n### November 2025 -- JCPOA Officially Declared Dead\\n\\nNovember 12, 2025 -- After months of fruitless backchannel negotiations, the European Union's foreign policy chief formally declared the [Joint Comprehensive Plan of Action (JCPOA](/glossary#jcpoa)) \\\"no longer operative.\\\" The 2015 nuclear deal, which the US had withdrawn from under President Trump's first term in 2018, had been on life support for years. Its official death removed the last multilateral framework constraining [Iran](/countries/iran)'s nuclear program.\\n\\nNovember 20, 2025 -- The [IAEA](/glossary#iaea) Director General reported that [Iran](/countries/iran) had denied inspectors access to two undisclosed sites flagged by Western intelligence. The agency's ability to verify the peaceful nature of Iran's nuclear activities was described as \\\"seriously compromised.\\\"\\n\\n### December 2025 -- Intelligence Warnings and Military Preparations\\n\\nDecember 5, 2025 -- The Israeli government publicly accused [Iran](/countries/iran) of conducting weapons-design work at a previously unknown facility south of Isfahan. [Israel](/countries/israel) shared satellite imagery with allied intelligence agencies, though Iran dismissed the claims as fabricated.\\n\\nDecember 18, 2025 -- US intelligence agencies delivered a classified briefing to the White House assessing that [Iran](/countries/iran) was \\\"within months\\\" of possessing the technical capability to assemble a nuclear device. The briefing was leaked to media outlets within days, dramatically escalating public alarm.\\n\\nDecember 30, 2025 -- President Trump issued a public warning that the [United States](/countries/united-states) \\\"will not allow [Iran](/countries/iran) to become a nuclear power under any circumstances.\\\" The statement was widely interpreted as laying the political groundwork for military action.\\n\\n## Phase 2: First Strikes (January 2026)\\n\\nThe transition from diplomatic pressure to kinetic action happened faster than most analysts predicted.\\n\\n### Early January -- Israeli Strikes on Nuclear Sites\\n\\nJanuary 8, 2026 -- [Israel](/countries/israel) launched a coordinated air campaign targeting [Iran](/countries/iran)'s nuclear infrastructure. F-35I Adir stealth fighters, supported by US intelligence and aerial refueling, struck the Fordow [enrichment](/glossary#enrichment) facility, the Isfahan uranium conversion plant, and [centrifuge](/glossary#centrifuge) production workshops at Natanz.\\n\\nThe strikes used US-supplied [GBU-57](/glossary#gbu-57) Massive Ordnance Penetrators -- the only munitions capable of reaching Fordow's underground chambers. [Iran](/countries/iran)'s air defenses, degraded by preceding electronic warfare operations, failed to intercept the majority of incoming strikes.\\n\\nJanuary 10, 2026 -- [Iran](/countries/iran) confirmed \\\"significant damage\\\" to nuclear facilities but insisted that its program remained intact. From the collapse of diplomacy in late 2025 through Israeli strikes, the US launch of [Operation Epic Fury](/articles/us-military-buildup-middle-east-operation-epic-fury), the [assassination of Supreme Leader Khamenei](/articles/iran-supreme-leader-khamenei-killed-us-strikes), and Iran's [retaliatory strikes on US bases](/articles/iran-retaliatory-strikes-us-bases-persian-gulf), the crisis has pushed the world closer to nuclear conflict than at any point since the Cuban Missile Crisis.\n\nThis timeline tracks every major event, organized by phase, so readers can understand how each step led to the next.\n\nFor core concepts referenced throughout this timeline, see [What Is Nuclear Breakout Time](/explainers/what-is-nuclear-breakout-time)?, [What Is the IAEA](/explainers/what-is-the-iaea)?, and [What Are Proxy Wars?](/explainers/what-are-proxy-wars).\n\n## Phase 1: Diplomatic Collapse (October -- December 2025)\n\nThe groundwork for the 2026 [Iran](/countries/iran) war was laid months before the first missile launched. A series of diplomatic failures and intelligence revelations closed the remaining offramps.\n\n### October 2025 -- IAEA Raises the Alarm on Enrichment\n\nOctober 14, 2025 -- The [International Atomic Energy Agency (IAEA](/glossary#iaea)) published a quarterly report confirming that [Iran](/countries/iran) had accelerated [uranium enrichment](/glossary#enrichment) at its Fordow underground facility. Inspectors documented stockpiles enriched to 60% purity -- a short technical step from the 90% required for weapons-grade material. The IAEA Board of Governors issued a formal rebuke, but no binding action followed.\n\nOctober 28, 2025 -- [Iran](/countries/iran) announced expanded [centrifuge](/glossary#centrifuge) cascades at Natanz, effectively doubling [enrichment](/glossary#enrichment) capacity. [Breakout time](/glossary#breakout-time) -- the period needed to produce enough [fissile material](/glossary#fissile-material) for a single weapon -- was assessed at under two weeks by multiple Western intelligence agencies.\n\n### November 2025 -- JCPOA Officially Declared Dead\n\nNovember 12, 2025 -- After months of fruitless backchannel negotiations, the European Union's foreign policy chief formally declared the [Joint Comprehensive Plan of Action (JCPOA](/glossary#jcpoa)) \"no longer operative.\" The 2015 nuclear deal, which the US had withdrawn from under President Trump's first term in 2018, had been on life support for years. Its official death removed the last multilateral framework constraining [Iran](/countries/iran)'s nuclear program.\n\nNovember 20, 2025 -- The [IAEA](/glossary#iaea) Director General reported that [Iran](/countries/iran) had denied inspectors access to two undisclosed sites flagged by Western intelligence. The agency's ability to verify the peaceful nature of Iran's nuclear activities was described as \"seriously compromised.\"\n\n### December 2025 -- Intelligence Warnings and Military Preparations\n\nDecember 5, 2025 -- The Israeli government publicly accused [Iran](/countries/iran) of conducting weapons-design work at a previously unknown facility south of Isfahan. [Israel](/countries/israel) shared satellite imagery with allied intelligence agencies, though Iran dismissed the claims as fabricated.\n\nDecember 18, 2025 -- US intelligence agencies delivered a classified briefing to the White House assessing that [Iran](/countries/iran) was \"within months\" of possessing the technical capability to assemble a nuclear device. The briefing was leaked to media outlets within days, dramatically escalating public alarm.\n\nDecember 30, 2025 -- President Trump issued a public warning that the [United States](/countries/united-states) \"will not allow [Iran](/countries/iran) to become a nuclear power under any circumstances.\" The statement was widely interpreted as laying the political groundwork for military action.\n\n## Phase 2: First Strikes (January 2026)\n\nThe transition from diplomatic pressure to kinetic action happened faster than most analysts predicted.\n\n### Early January -- Israeli Strikes on Nuclear Sites\n\nJanuary 8, 2026 -- [Israel](/countries/israel) launched a coordinated air campaign targeting [Iran](/countries/iran)'s nuclear infrastructure. [Iran](/countries/iran)'s air defenses, degraded by preceding electronic warfare operations, failed to intercept the majority of incoming strikes.\n\nJanuary 10, 2026 -- [Iran](/countries/iran) confirmed \"significant damage\" to nuclear facilities but insisted that its program remained intact. No provider-specific `discord` tool exposed to the agent.\n\n## Musts\n\n- Always: `channel: \"discord\"`.\n- Respect gating: `channels.discord.actions.*` (some default off: `roles`, `moderation`, `presence`, `channels`).\n- Prefer explicit ids: `guildId`, `channelId`, `messageId`, `userId`.\n- Multi-account: optional `accountId`.\n\n## Guidelines\n\n- Avoid Markdown tables in outbound Discord messages.\n- Mention users as `<@USER_ID>`.\n- Prefer Discord components v2 (`components`) for rich UI; use legacy `embeds` only when you must.\n\n## Targets\n\n- Send-like actions: `to: \"channel:<id>\"` or `to: \"user:<id>\"`.\n- Message-specific actions: `channelId: \"<id>\"` (or `to`) + `messageId: \"<id>\"`.\n\n## Common Actions (Examples)\n\nSend message:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"send\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"to\": \"channel:123\",\n  \"message\": \"hello\",\n  \"silent\": true\n}\n```\n\nSend with media:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"send\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"to\": \"channel:123\",\n  \"message\": \"see attachment\",\n  \"media\": \"file:///tmp/example.png\"\n}\n```\n\n- Optional `silent: true` to suppress Discord notifications.\n\nSend with components v2 (recommended for rich UI):\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"send\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"to\": \"channel:123\",\n  \"message\": \"Status update\",\n  \"components\": \"[Carbon v2 components]\"\n}\n```\n\n- `components` expects Carbon component instances (Container, TextDisplay, etc.) from JS/TS integrations.\n- Do not combine `components` with `embeds` (Discord rejects v2 + embeds).\n\nLegacy embeds (not recommended):\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"send\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"to\": \"channel:123\",\n  \"message\": \"Status update\",\n  \"embeds\": [{ \"title\": \"Legacy\", \"description\": \"Embeds are legacy.\" }]\n}\n```\n\n- `embeds` are ignored when components v2 are present.\n\nReact:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"react\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"channelId\": \"123\",\n  \"messageId\": \"456\",\n  \"emoji\": \"✅\"\n}\n```\n\nRead:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"read\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"to\": \"channel:123\",\n  \"limit\": 20\n}\n```\n\nEdit / delete:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"edit\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"channelId\": \"123\",\n  \"messageId\": \"456\",\n  \"message\": \"fixed typo\"\n}\n```\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"delete\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"channelId\": \"123\",\n  \"messageId\": \"456\"\n}\n```\n\nPoll:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"poll\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"to\": \"channel:123\",\n  \"pollQuestion\": \"Lunch?\",\n  \"pollOption\": [\"Pizza\", \"Sushi\", \"Salad\"],\n  \"pollMulti\": false,\n  \"pollDurationHours\": 24\n}\n```\n\nPins:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"pin\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"channelId\": \"123\",\n triage\"\n}\n```\n\nSearch:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"search\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"guildId\": \"999\",\n  \"query\": \"release notes\",\n  \"channelIds\": [\"123\", \"456\"],\n A series of diplomatic failures and intelligence revelations closed the remaining offramps.\\n\\n### October 2025 -- IAEA Raises the Alarm on Enrichment\\n\\nOctober 14, 2025 -- The [International Atomic Energy Agency (IAEA](/glossary#iaea)) published a quarterly report confirming that [Iran](/countries/iran) had accelerated [uranium enrichment](/glossary#enrichment) at its Fordow underground facility. Inspectors documented stockpiles enriched to 60% purity -- a short technical step from the 90% required for weapons-grade material. The IAEA Board of Governors issued a formal rebuke, but no binding action followed.\\n\\nOctober 28, 2025 -- [Iran](/countries/iran) announced expanded [centrifuge](/glossary#centrifuge) cascades at Natanz, effectively doubling [enrichment](/glossary#enrichment) capacity. [Breakout time](/glossary#breakout-time) -- the period needed to produce enough [fissile material](/glossary#fissile-material) for a single weapon -- was assessed at under two weeks by multiple Western intelligence agencies.\\n\\n### November 2025 -- JCPOA Officially Declared Dead\\n\\nNovember 12, 2025 -- After months of fruitless backchannel negotiations, the European Union's foreign policy chief formally declared the [Joint Comprehensive Plan of Action (JCPOA](/glossary#jcpoa)) \\\"no longer operative.\\\" The 2015 nuclear deal, which the US had withdrawn from under President Trump's first term in 2018, had been on life support for years. Its official death removed the last multilateral framework constraining [Iran](/countries/iran)'s nuclear program.\\n\\nNovember 20, 2025 -- The [IAEA](/glossary#iaea) Director General reported that [Iran](/countries/iran) had denied inspectors access to two undisclosed sites flagged by Western intelligence. The agency's ability to verify the peaceful nature of Iran's nuclear activities was described as \\\"seriously compromised.\\\"\\n\\n### December 2025 -- Intelligence Warnings and Military Preparations\\n\\nDecember 5, 2025 -- The Israeli government publicly accused [Iran](/countries/iran) of conducting weapons-design work at a previously unknown facility south of Isfahan. [Israel](/countries/israel) shared satellite imagery with allied intelligence agencies, though Iran dismissed the claims as fabricated.\\n\\nDecember 18, 2025 -- US intelligence agencies delivered a classified briefing to the White House assessing that [Iran](/countries/iran) was \\\"within months\\\" of possessing the technical capability to assemble a nuclear device. The briefing was leaked to media outlets within days, dramatically escalating public alarm.\\n\\nDecember 30, 2025 -- President Trump issued a public warning that the [United States](/countries/united-states) \\\"will not allow [Iran](/countries/iran) to become a nuclear power under any circumstances.\\\" The statement was widely interpreted as laying the political groundwork for military action.\\n\\n## Phase 2: First Strikes (January 2026)\\n\\nThe transition from diplomatic pressure to kinetic action happened faster than most analysts predicted.\\n\\n### Early January -- Israeli Strikes on Nuclear Sites\\n\\nJanuary 8, 2026 -- [Israel](/countries/israel) launched a coordinated air campaign targeting [Iran](/countries/iran)'s nuclear infrastructure. F-35I Adir stealth fighters, supported by US intelligence and aerial refueling, struck the Fordow [enrichment](/glossary#enrichment) facility, the Isfahan uranium conversion plant, and [centrifuge](/glossary#centrifuge) production workshops at Natanz.\\n\\nThe strikes used US-supplied [GBU-57](/glossary#gbu-57) Massive Ordnance Penetrators -- the only munitions capable of reaching Fordow's underground chambers. [Iran](/countries/iran)'s air defenses, degraded by preceding electronic warfare operations, failed to intercept the majority of incoming strikes.\\n\\nJanuary 10, 2026 -- [Iran](/countries/iran) confirmed \\\"significant damage\\\" to nuclear facilities but insisted that its program remained intact. The briefing was leaked to media outlets within days, dramatically escalating public alarm.\n\nDecember 30, 2025 -- President Trump issued a public warning that the [United States](/countries/united-states) \"will not allow [Iran](/countries/iran) to become a nuclear power under any circumstances.\" The statement was widely interpreted as laying the political groundwork for military action.\n\n## Phase 2: First Strikes (January 2026)\n\nThe transition from diplomatic pressure to kinetic action happened faster than most analysts predicted.\n\n### Early January -- Israeli Strikes on Nuclear Sites\n\nJanuary 8, 2026 -- [Israel](/countries/israel) launched a coordinated air campaign targeting [Iran](/countries/iran)'s nuclear infrastructure. F-35I Adir stealth fighters, supported by US intelligence and aerial refueling, struck the Fordow [enrichment](/glossary#enrichment) facility, the Isfahan uranium conversion plant, and [centrifuge](/glossary#centrifuge) production workshops at Natanz.\n\nThe strikes used US-supplied [GBU-57](/glossary#gbu-57) Massive Ordnance Penetrators -- the only munitions capable of reaching Fordow's underground chambers. [Iran](/countries/iran)'s air defenses, degraded by preceding electronic warfare operations, failed to intercept the majority of incoming strikes.\n\nJanuary 10, 2026 -- [Iran](/countries/iran) confirmed \"significant damage\" to nuclear facilities but insisted that its program remained intact. The [IRGC](/glossary#irgc) described the strikes as \"an act of war requiring a decisive response.\"\n\n### Mid-January -- Iran Retaliates Against US Assets\n\nJanuary 15, 2026 -- [Iran](/countries/iran) launched its first retaliatory strikes, firing over 40 ballistic missiles at US military facilities in Iraq and the UAE. Three missiles struck Al Asad Air Base in western Iraq. US [Patriot](/glossary#patriot) and [THAAD](/glossary#thaad) missile defense systems intercepted the majority of incoming projectiles, but several base structures sustained damage.\n\nJanuary 18, 2026 -- Iranian-backed militias in Iraq launched coordinated drone and rocket attacks against the US Embassy compound in Baghdad's Green Zone. No American diplomats were killed, but the attacks forced a partial evacuation of non-essential personnel.\n\nJanuary 22, 2026 -- Houthi forces in Yemen, acting in coordination with [Iran](/countries/iran), launched anti-ship cruise missiles at a US Navy destroyer transiting the Bab el-Mandeb Strait. The missiles were intercepted, but the attack demonstrated Iran's ability to threaten maritime chokepoints far from its borders.\n\n## Phase 3: Operation Epic Fury (February 2026)\n\nFebruary marked the transformation of targeted strikes into a full-scale military campaign.\n\n### Early February -- US Launches Operation Epic Fury\n\nFebruary 3, 2026 -- President Trump announced the commencement of Operation Epic Fury, describing it as a campaign to \"permanently eliminate [Iran](/countries/iran)'s ability to threaten the [United States](/countries/united-states), our allies, and the world with nuclear weapons.\" The Pentagon confirmed the deployment of two [carrier strike groups](/glossary#carrier-strike-group) to the Persian Gulf and Arabian Sea.\n\nFebruary 7, 2026 -- B-2 Spirit stealth bombers, operating from Diego Garcia, conducted the first US strikes on Iranian military command-and-control facilities in Tehran. messages.\n- Mention users as `<@USER_ID>`.\n- Prefer Discord components v2 (`components`) for rich UI; use legacy `embeds` only when you must.\n\n## Targets\n\n- Send-like actions: `to: \"channel:<id>\"` or `to: \"user:<id>\"`.\n- Message-specific actions: `channelId: \"<id>\"` (or `to`) + `messageId: \"<id>\"`.\n\n## Common Actions (Examples)\n\nSend message:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"send\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"to\": \"channel:123\",\n  \"message\": \"hello\",\n  \"silent\": true\n}\n```\n\nSend with media:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"send\",\n notifications.\n\nSend with components v2 (recommended for rich UI):\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"send\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"to\": \"channel:123\",\n  \"message\": \"Status update\",\n  \"components\": \"[Carbon v2 components]\"\n}\n```\n\n- `components` expects Carbon component instances (Container, TextDisplay, etc.) from JS/TS integrations.\n- Do not combine `components` with `embeds` (Discord rejects v2 + embeds).\n\nLegacy embeds (not recommended):\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"send\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"to\": \"channel:123\",\n present.\n\nReact:\n\n```json\n{\n  \"action\": \"react\",\n  \"channel\": \"discord\",\n  \"channelId\": \"123\",\n  \"messageId\": \"456\",\n  \"emoji\": \"✅\"\n}\n```\n\nRead:\n\n```json\n{\n From the collapse of diplomacy in late 2025 through Israeli strikes, the US launch of [Operation Epic Fury](/articles/us-military-buildup-middle-east-operation-epic-fury), the [assassination of Supreme Leader Khamenei](/articles/iran-supreme-leader-khamenei-killed-us-strikes), and Iran's [retaliatory strikes on US bases](/articles/iran-retaliatory-strikes-us-bases-persian-gulf), the crisis has pushed the world closer to nuclear conflict than at any point since the Cuban Missile Crisis.\\n\\nThis timeline tracks every major event, organized by phase, so readers can understand how each step led to the next.\\n\\nFor core concepts referenced throughout this timeline, see [What Is Nuclear Breakout Time](/explainers/what-is-nuclear-breakout-time)?, [What Is the IAEA](/explainers/what-is-the-iaea)?, and [What Are Proxy Wars?](/explainers/what-are-proxy-wars).\\n\\n## Phase 1: Diplomatic Collapse (October -- December 2025)\\n\\nThe groundwork for the 2026 [Iran](/countries/iran) war was laid months before the first missile launched. A series of diplomatic failures and intelligence revelations closed the remaining offramps.\\n\\n### October 2025 -- IAEA Raises the Alarm on Enrichment\\n\\nOctober 14, 2025 -- The [International Atomic Energy Agency (IAEA](/glossary#iaea)) published a quarterly report confirming that [Iran](/countries/iran) had accelerated [uranium enrichment](/glossary#enrichment) at its Fordow underground facility. Inspectors documented stockpiles enriched to 60% purity -- a short technical step from the 90% required for weapons-grade material. The IAEA Board of Governors issued a formal rebuke, but no binding action followed.\\n\\nOctober 28, 2025 -- [Iran](/countries/iran) announced expanded [centrifuge](/glossary#centrifuge) cascades at Natanz, effectively doubling [enrichment](/glossary#enrichment) capacity. [Breakout time](/glossary#breakout-time) -- the period needed to produce enough [fissile material](/glossary#fissile-material) for a single weapon -- was assessed at under two weeks by multiple Western intelligence agencies.\\n\\n### November 2025 -- JCPOA Officially Declared Dead\\n\\nNovember 12, 2025 -- After months of fruitless backchannel negotiations, the European Union's foreign policy chief formally declared the [Joint Comprehensive Plan of Action (JCPOA](/glossary#jcpoa)) \\\"no longer operative.\\\" The 2015 nuclear deal, which the US had withdrawn from under President Trump's first term in 2018, had been on life support for years. Its official death removed the last multilateral framework constraining [Iran](/countries/iran)'s nuclear program.\\n\\nNovember 20, 2025 -- The [IAEA](/glossary#iaea) Director General reported that [Iran](/countries/iran) had denied inspectors access to two undisclosed sites flagged by Western intelligence. The agency's ability to verify the peaceful nature of Iran's nuclear activities was described as \\\"seriously compromised.\\\"\\n\\n### December 2025 -- Intelligence Warnings and Military Preparations\\n\\nDecember 5, 2025 -- The Israeli government publicly accused [Iran](/countries/iran) of conducting weapons-design work at a previously unknown facility south of Isfahan. [Israel](/countries/israel) shared satellite imagery with allied intelligence agencies, though Iran dismissed the claims as fabricated.\\n\\nDecember 18, 2025 -- US intelligence agencies delivered a classified briefing to the White House assessing that [Iran](/countries/iran) was \\\"within months\\\" of possessing the technical capability to assemble a nuclear device. The briefing was leaked to media outlets within days, dramatically escalating public alarm.\\n\\nDecember 30, 2025 -- President Trump issued a public warning that the [United States](/countries/united-states) \\\"will not allow [Iran](/countries/iran) to become a nuclear power under any circumstances.\\\" The statement was widely interpreted as laying the political groundwork for military action.\\n\\n## Phase 2: First Strikes (January 2026)\\n\\nThe transition from diplomatic pressure to kinetic action happened faster than most analysts predicted.\\n\\n### Early January -- Israeli Strikes on Nuclear Sites\\n\\nJanuary 8, 2026 -- [Israel](/countries/israel) launched a coordinated air campaign targeting [Iran](/countries/iran)'s nuclear infrastructure. F-35I Adir stealth fighters, supported by US intelligence and aerial refueling, struck the Fordow [enrichment](/glossary#enrichment) facility, the Isfahan uranium conversion plant, and [centrifuge](/glossary#centrifuge) production workshops at Natanz.\\n\\nThe strikes used US-supplied [GBU-57](/glossary#gbu-57) Massive Ordnance Penetrators -- the only munitions capable of reaching Fordow's underground chambers. [Iran](/countries/iran)'s air defenses, degraded by preceding electronic warfare operations, failed to intercept the majority of incoming strikes.\\n\\nJanuary 10, 2026 -- [Iran](/countries/iran) confirmed \\\"significant damage\\\" to nuclear facilities but insisted that its program remained intact. The [IRGC](/glossary#irgc) described the strikes as \\\"an act of war requiring a decisive response.\\\"\\n\\n###\\n<<<END_EXTERNAL_UNTRUSTED_CONTENT id=\\\"6c9a55fa16a56c97\\\">>>\"\n}"

The IAEA Board of Governors issued a formal rebuke, but no binding action followed.\\n\\nOctober 28, 2025 -- [Iran](/countries/iran) announced expanded [centrifuge](/glossary#centrifuge) cascades at Natanz, effectively doubling [enrichment](/glossary#enrichment) capacity. [Breakout time](/glossary#breakout-time) -- the period needed to produce enough [fissile material](/glossary#fissile-material) for a single weapon -- was assessed at under two weeks by multiple Western intelligence agencies.\\n\\n### November 2025 -- JCPOA Officially Declared Dead\\n\\nNovember 12, 2025 -- After months of fruitless backchannel negotiations, the European Union's foreign policy chief formally declared the [Joint Comprehensive Plan of Action (JCPOA](/glossary#jcpoa)) \\\"no longer operative.\\\" The 2015 nuclear deal, which the US had withdrawn from under President Trump's first term in 2018, had been on life support for years. Its official death removed the last multilateral framework constraining [Iran](/countries/iran)'s nuclear program.\\n\\nNovember 20, 2025 -- The [IAEA](/glossary#iaea) Director General reported that [Iran](/countries/iran) had denied inspectors access to two undisclosed sites flagged by Western intelligence. The agency's ability to verify the peaceful nature of Iran's nuclear activities was described as \\\"seriously compromised.\\\"\\n\\n### December 2025 -- Intelligence Warnings and Military Preparations\\n\\nDecember 5, 2025 -- The Israeli government publicly accused [Iran](/countries/iran) of conducting weapons-design work at a previously unknown facility south of Isfahan. [Israel](/countries/israel) shared satellite imagery with allied intelligence agencies, though Iran dismissed the claims as fabricated.\\n\\nDecember 18, 2025 -- US intelligence agencies delivered a classified briefing to the White House assessing that [Iran](/countries/iran) was \\\"within months\\\" of possessing the technical capability to assemble a nuclear device. The briefing was leaked to media outlets within days, dramatically escalating public alarm.\\n\\nDecember 30, 2025 -- President Trump issued a public warning that the [United States](/countries/united-states) \\\"will not allow [Iran](/countries/iran) to become a nuclear power under any circumstances.\\\" The statement was widely interpreted as laying the political groundwork for military action.\\n\\n## Phase 2: First Strikes (January 2026)\\n\\nThe transition from diplomatic pressure to kinetic action happened faster than most analysts predicted.\\n\\n### Early January -- Israeli Strikes on Nuclear Sites\\n\\nJanuary 8, 2026 -- [Israel](/countries/israel) launched a coordinated air campaign targeting [Iran](/countries/iran)'s nuclear infrastructure. F-35I Adir stealth fighters, supported by US intelligence and aerial refueling, struck the Fordow [enrichment](/glossary#enrichment) facility, the Isfahan uranium conversion plant, and [centrifuge](/glossary#centrifuge) production workshops at Natanz.\\n\\nThe strikes used US-supplied [GBU-57](/glossary#gbu-57) Massive Ordnance Penetrators -- the only munitions capable of reaching Fordow's underground chambers. [Iran](/countries/iran)'s air defenses, degraded by preceding electronic warfare operations, failed to intercept the majority of incoming strikes.\\n\\nJanuary 10, 2026 -- [Iran](/countries/iran) confirmed \\\"significant damage\\\" to nuclear facilities but insisted that its program remained intact. The [IRGC](/glossary#irgc) described the strikes as \\\"an act of war requiring a decisive response.\\\"\\n\\n### Mid-January -- Iran Retaliates Against US Assets\\n\\nJanuary 15, 2026 -- [Iran](/countries/iran) launched its first retaliatory strikes, firing over 40 ballistic missiles at US military facilities in Iraq and the UAE. Three missiles struck Al Asad Air Base in western Iraq. US [Patriot](/glossary#patriot) and [THAAD](/glossary#thaad) missile defense systems intercepted the majority of incoming projectiles, but several base structures sustained damage.\\n\\nJanuary 18, 2026 -- Iranian-backed militias in Iraq launched coordinated drone and rocket attacks against the US Embassy compound in Baghdad's Green Zone. No American diplomats were killed, but the attacks forced a partial evacuation of non-essential personnel.\\n\\nJanuary 22, 2026 -- Houthi forces in Yemen, acting in coordination with [Iran](/countries/iran), launched anti-ship cruise missiles at a US Navy destroyer transiting the Bab el-Mandeb Strait. The missiles were intercepted, but the attack demonstrated Iran's ability to threaten maritime chokepoints far from its borders.\\n\\n## Phase 3: Operation Epic Fury (February 2026)\\n\\nFebruary marked the transformation of targeted strikes into a full-scale military campaign.\\n\\n### Early February -- US Launches Operation Epic Fury\\n\\nFebruary 3, 2026 -- President Trump announced the commencement of Operation Epic Fury, describing it as a campaign to \\\"permanently eliminate [Iran](/countries/iran)'s ability to threaten the [United States](/countries/united-states), our allies, and the world with nuclear weapons.\\\" The Pentagon confirmed the deployment of two [carrier strike groups](/glossary#carrier-strike-group) to the Persian Gulf and Arabian Sea.\\n\\nFebruary 7, 2026 -- B-2 Spirit stealth bombers, operating from Diego Garcia, conducted the first US strikes on Iranian military command-and-control facilities in Tehran. The strikes targeted [IRGC](/glossary#irgc) headquarters, air defense networks, and ballistic missile production facilities.\\n\\nFebruary 10, 2026 -- US forces in the region s\\n<<<END_EXTERNAL_UNTRUSTED_CONTENT id=\\\"5fad578a71627fb8\\\">>>\"\n}"
